## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Component
    participant ActionCreator
    participant Dispatch
    participant LadsReducer
    participant API
    participant Store
    
    Component->>ActionCreator: updateLadLabel(lad, newLabel)
    ActionCreator->>Dispatch: dispatch UPDATE_LAD_LABEL
    Dispatch->>LadsReducer: action.payload {lad, newLabel}
    LadsReducer->>LadsReducer: Map and update lad_name
    LadsReducer->>Store: Update state with new lads array
    ActionCreator->>API: PUT /location/lads/:id {lad_name}
    API-->>ActionCreator: Success response
    Store-->>Component: Updated state
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class LadsDuck {
        +String mountPoint
        +Object actionTypes
        +Object actionCreators
        +Object selectors
        +Function reducer
    }
    
    class ActionCreators {
        +fetchLads()
        +updateLadLabel(lad, newLabel)
    }
    
    class Selectors {
        +getLadsList(state)
        +selectLadsListAlphabetically(state)
        +selectGroupedLads(state)
    }
    
    class LadsReducer {
        +UPDATE_LAD_LABEL
        +handle state updates
    }
    
    class DuckReducer {
        +fetch actions
        +handle API state
    }
    
    LadsDuck --> ActionCreators
    LadsDuck --> Selectors
    LadsDuck --> LadsReducer
    LadsDuck --> DuckReducer
    
    ActionCreators --> axios
    Selectors --> lodash
    Selectors --> reselect
```
